369.107 Legal recognition of electronic records, electronic signatures, and
electronic contracts.
(1) A record or signature may not be denied legal effect orenforceability solely because
it is in electronic form.
(2') A contract may not bc denied legal effect or enforceability solely because an
eleclronic record was used in its bnnalion.
(3) Tf a law requires a record to he iii writing, an electi-onie record satisfies the law.
(4) If a law requires a signature, an clcctronic signature satisfies the law.
Elective: August 1,2000
Hi,li,ry: Created 2001) Ky. Aclx ch. 3(H, Hec. 7, ellactive Augu>! 1,2000.

Arrival Information 
Subjective 
Patient is a 33 year old female that presents status post L distal radius fracture (ORIF). Although she is right handed, she notes that 
she is has difficulty with gripping, lifting, wrist ROM, and global use of her LUE. She notes that on 12/5 she was working at Sonic 
when she misstopped and had a FOOSH injury. She had surgery on 12/7 and will follow up on 1/30. She notes that she is unable to 
move her fingers well secondary to swelling and N/T into 3-4 finger going up into the outside of her elbow. She is now sleeping in 
her bed but has been sleeping on the couch due to discomfort.

Assessment 
Assessment 
The pleasant 33 y/o female patient appears before physical therapy this date with reports of L wrist stiffness, loss of ROM, 
decreased use for ADL's and IADL's secondary to decreased dexterity and strength, as well as N/T in ulnar aspect distribution. 
Upon assessment, the patient's s/s are consistent with status post L ORIF of radius. Patient presents with moderate swelling and 
severe limitations in ROM, mobility, and decreased arthrokinematics of elbow and wrist five weeks post op. Concerns regarding 
end ranges of elbow flexion, supination, as well as global mobility of MCP's + wrist. The patient is appropriate for and would 
benefit from skilled physical therapy to address deficits listed above. The patient was educated on and is in agreement with the 
goals established and the physical therapy plan of care to ensue. The patient consents to physical therapy treatment. There are 
no contraindications to beginning physical therapy at this time.

Good potential to reach and maintain prior level of function

Long Term Goals

Assessment 
The pleasant 33 y/o female patient appears before physical therapy this date with reports of L wrist stiffness, loss of ROM, 
decreased use for ADL's and IADL's secondary to decreased dexterity and strength, as well as N/T in ulnar aspect distribution. 
Upon assessment, the patient's s/s are consistent with status post L ORIF of radius. Patient presents with moderate swelling and 
severe limitations in ROM, mobility, and decreased arthrokinematics of elbow and wrist five weeks post op. Concerns regarding 
end ranges of elbow flexion, supination, as well as global mobility of MCP's + wrist. The patient is appropriate for and would 
benefit from skilled physical therapy to address deficits listed above. The patient was educated on and is in agreement with the 
goals established and the physical therapy plan of care to ensue. The patient consents to physical therapy treatment. There are 
no contraindications to beginning physical therapy at this time.
